        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2111107844" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12340195896072197872"><b>Reread: 10th June 2018<br/><br/>So much raw emotions and honesty. It was like using a magnifying glass and analyzing the two very hearts and souls of these two imperfectly perfect couple. *happy sigh* 😌 Laurent and Damianos will always have a place in my heart. 😍<br/><br/><br/><br/>Original review: Revised edition<br/><br/>I don't want this to end .. I really don't. 😭 And I'm quite sad that I've finished book two and now there's only one book left in this trilogy. These books are simply just too awesome! 👏<br/><br/>In the first book, we learnt </b></span>
  <span id="freeText12340195896072197872" style="display:none"><b>Reread: 10th June 2018<br><br>So much raw emotions and honesty. It was like using a magnifying glass and analyzing the two very hearts and souls of these two imperfectly perfect couple. *happy sigh* 😌 Laurent and Damianos will always have a place in my heart. 😍<br><br><br><br>Original review: Revised edition<br><br>I don't want this to end .. I really don't. 😭 And I'm quite sad that I've finished book two and now there's only one book left in this trilogy. These books are simply just too awesome! 👏<br><br>In the first book, we learnt about the clashes between two countries and our two protagonists, and Damen having to live as a slave in Veretian court . The second book is about Laurent and Damen's journey to the border to escape from the hands of the evil regent and to achieve what's rightfully theirs. It's just a fantastic read! I can't help but slowly and irrevocably falling in love in Laurent since he's such a mysterious, intricate and intelligent character. ❤️ It's very enticing to see how two people from poles apart gradually falling in love with each other. I love that Damen is such a caring, protective angel character. He was exactly the person that can cure and pick apart the broken pieces of Laurent’s traumatic childhood. And when Laurent finally lowered his guards and gave in to Damen, let's just say, I was a happy puddled good on the floor with silly swooning smiles! 😁😍<br><br>Laurent really is such an enigmatic and smart person. No one but Laurent would have thought about using a simple sapphire earrings to disguise himself. And I'm sure the UST between these two couple could light up the sleeping town of Nesson Eloy. He's not all frigid and uptight, our Laurent has a fun and mischievous side to it and Damen witnessed it for the first time. 😉<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1528618051i/25706366._SY540_.jpg" width="height=" alt="description/" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1528617516i/25706197._SY540_.jpg" width="height=" alt="description/" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And the moment when Laurent asked Damen for the other piece of slave wrist cuff for keeping is hands down one of the most romantic moments of all times. 😍😌 And that first kiss and the first time they made love? No wonder why this book became a classic MM romance novel. 😱<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1528617516i/25706195._SY540_.jpg" width="height=" alt="description/" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1528617516i/25706199._SY540_.jpg" width="height=" alt="description/" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And he said, "one night and one morning". And he'd leave quietly and discreetly without rousing Damen because he didn't wanna say goodbye. Goodbyes are not Laurent's style. 😭<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1528617516i/25706198._SY540_.jpg" width="height=" alt="description/" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And we have two heartbreaking moments in this book too. 💔 The death of one who's precious to Laurent and the one who pretended loyal to him. Both were heart-wrenching and agonizing. But in the end, these two innocent souls were puppeteered and manipulated by sick bastard regent. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1528617516i/25706200.jpg" width="height=" alt="description/" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>There you have it all, the drama, the romance, the excitement, suspense, the politics, the enigmas, that bittersweet angst and the hopes and dreams. 😌<br><br>I really have to admit that I was quite skeptical when I first read this trilogy and I didn't think I'd love these book as much as I do now. I even felt they were a bit overrated since this trilogy is described as a world phenomenal series. Boy boy boy .. how wrong I was! 😏 These two really really grew on me and made me fall in love with them. 💙<br><br>I can't wait to read the third book. And at the same time, I'm dragging to read that one because that would be the end of these two. How everything will fold out and how Laurent will outsmart everyone? We only need to read "Kings Rising" to find out the truth. 😉😘<br><br><br>5 But you are mine now. You are still my slave tonight stars</b><br>⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️<br><br><b>
  <i>PS. This is how I always imagined Laurent in my mind.</i>
</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1528618703i/25706422._SY540_.jpg" width="height=" alt="description/" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2435567399?book_show_action=true">Jun 25, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Hamad" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Hamad" href="/user/show/54464244-hamad">Hamad</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/54464244-hamad?shelf=2018-reads">2018-reads</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2435567399" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5980555753969628481">This review and other non-spoilery reviews can be found <a href='https://thebookprescription.wordpress.com/2018/07/02/captive-prince-vol-2-review/' rel='nofollow noopener'>@The Book Prescription</a><br/><br/><i>“I lack,” said Laurent, “the easy mannerisms that are usually shared with,” you could see him pushing the words out, “a lover.”<br/>“You lack the easy mannerisms that are usually shared with anyone,” said Damen.”</i><br/><br/>🌟 Prince’s Gambit is one of the best books I have read this year, if not ever!<br/>The author stepped up her game in all aspects of the story.<br/><br/>🌟 If you read this book or you are planning to, then we are past the controver</span>
  <span id="freeText5980555753969628481" style="display:none">This review and other non-spoilery reviews can be found <a href="https://thebookprescription.wordpress.com/2018/07/02/captive-prince-vol-2-review/" rel="nofollow noopener">@The Book Prescription</a><br /><br /><i>“I lack,” said Laurent, “the easy mannerisms that are usually shared with,” you could see him pushing the words out, “a lover.”<br />“You lack the easy mannerisms that are usually shared with anyone,” said Damen.”</i><br /><br />🌟 Prince’s Gambit is one of the best books I have read this year, if not ever!<br />The author stepped up her game in all aspects of the story.<br /><br />🌟 If you read this book or you are planning to, then we are past the controversy surrounding book 1 and we agree that we know what we are getting into when we are reading this. That being said, the improvements made me question myself if I was reading a book by the same author. And it is common that books that are 2nd in a series fall into the “Middle book syndrome” and they usually suck. But this had a mutation that made it even more superior.<br /><br />🌟 I said in my review of book 1 that it had good characters, average world building and plot. Now we get to discover more about the world, there is a map and there is traveling between different countries which gave a chance to expand the whole thing.<br /><br />🌟 And what about the sudden turn of events?! I was so thrilled and wanted to finish this to see what happens because there were all kinds of possibilities.<br /><br />🌟 This book is character driven and that is even more obvious now. I don’t like Inst-romance in books but this is the total opposite, Pacat is so good at writing a slow burn romance and I was like, just shut up and do something you too! And the good thing is that it all happens in a short number of pages but the struggle is real because we care about the characters.<br /><br />🌟 The writing style is as good as book 1 where it was the strongest point and made me continue the series, the world choices that Pacat use is so vast and unique and I totally like it!<br /><br /><i>“And if you want a personal message,” said Laurent, “You can tell my uncle boykiller that he can cut the head off every child from here to the capital. It won’t make him into a king, it will simply mean he has no one left to fuck.”</i><br /><br />🌟 Summary: Captive prince 2 is an even better book that the first installment and the story just keeps getting better, so if you like the series or you want to give it another chance then this book is the best reason to do so!<br /><br />🌟 Prescription: For fans of LGBT/ Historical fictions reads.</span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1541096940" />
    <a title="☆ Todd" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/12415682-todd"><img alt="☆ Todd" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1539502816p2/12415682.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1541096940?book_show_action=true">May 21, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="☆ Todd" class="user" itemprop="url" name="☆ Todd" href="/user/show/12415682-todd">☆ Todd</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1541096940" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7018711466010935057"><br/>*This* story is what I wanted more of in book 1. The setup in the first story was critical; however, here we finally get to see Damen and Laurent becoming a team. Building a strong, yet still fragile, trust.<br/><br/>Plus, the plotting and scheming in the first book didn't hold a candle to the underhanded planning carefully and precisely played out in book 2.<br/><br/>I do have to admit that these books continue to frustrate the shit out of my 'romance' heart, as getting moments of affection from Laurent are equiva</span>
  <span id="freeText7018711466010935057" style="display:none"><br />*This* story is what I wanted more of in book 1. The setup in the first story was critical; however, here we finally get to see Damen and Laurent becoming a team. Building a strong, yet still fragile, trust.<br /><br />Plus, the plotting and scheming in the first book didn't hold a candle to the underhanded planning carefully and precisely played out in book 2.<br /><br />I do have to admit that these books continue to frustrate the shit out of my 'romance' heart, as getting moments of affection from Laurent are equivalent to searching for an ocean in the middle of a desert.<br /><br />The end of book 2 was pretty much perfection on a silver platter, except that now I'm goddamn afraid to read book 3, with the entire fort being privy to Damen's true identity.<br /><br />Either Laurent has known the entire time, which I suspect, or we're going to see some Amy Lane level of angst happening, when Laurent has to work side by side, shoulder to shoulder with the man who killed his beloved older brother.<br /><br />Whatever the case may be, I'm sensing some high drama to come in book 3 and can't wait to see either Laurent or Damen finally chop the head off of the Regent's slimy, loathsome body.<br /><br />4.5 stars.<br /><br />-----------------------------------------------<br /><br /><b>** NOTE: For anyone interested, I found a truly incredible fan art site dedicated to the Captive Prince trilogy, so if you're a fan, do check it out. It's all kinds of amazing. : )<br /><br />--&gt; <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://kyroi.tumblr.com">https://kyroi.tumblr.com</a> </b><br /><br />-----------------------------------------------<br /><br /><b>Book 1 Review: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1540802754">https://www.goodreads.com/review/show...</a> </b><br /><br /><b>Book 3 Review: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1541096975">https://www.goodreads.com/review/show...</a> </b><br /><br /><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/list/12415682-todd?order=d&amp;sort=date_read&amp;view=reviews" rel="nofollow noopener">See All My Latest Reads (Review Quick-Links)</a><br /><br />-----------------------------------------------</span>

<div id="review_1576974354" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1576974354" />
    <a title="Kyle" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9740056-kyle"><img alt="Kyle" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1481754383p2/9740056.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1576974354?book_show_action=true">Oct 11, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kyle" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kyle" href="/user/show/9740056-kyle">Kyle</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook 9780987507334" href="/book/show/25270783-captive-prince">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1576974354" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15254893974392200230"><div><p>Much better than Volume One!</p> <p>I was a bit disappointed when I finished Volume One, but now having finished Volume Two I can see how it was simply a setup for Volume Two. With Laurent and Damen forced to trust each other in order to avoid a war between their two countries, a new sexual tension starts to build between the two of them. As the book progresses it gets to the point where you want to shout at the book, "oh just do it already!"</p><p>The complex plot is great as Laurent tries to outwit his uncl</p></div></span>
  <span id="freeText15254893974392200230" style="display:none"><div><p>Much better than Volume One!</p> <p>I was a bit disappointed when I finished Volume One, but now having finished Volume Two I can see how it was simply a setup for Volume Two. With Laurent and Damen forced to trust each other in order to avoid a war between their two countries, a new sexual tension starts to build between the two of them. As the book progresses it gets to the point where you want to shout at the book, "oh just do it already!"</p><p>The complex plot is great as Laurent tries to outwit his uncle. Of course, Damen continues to avoid getting found out as the Prince who killed Laurent's older brother. All the twists and turns are great. It certainly kept me guessing what would happen next and I LOVE that about a book.</p><p>If there was any negative about the book it would be the huge cliffhanger that it ended on! Now where's my copy of book 3?</p><br /></div></span>
  <a data-text-id="15254893974392200230" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_482216963" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/482216963" />
    <a title="Kat" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4878104-kat"><img alt="Kat" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1515345527p2/4878104.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/482216963?book_show_action=true">Dec 21, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kat" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kat" href="/user/show/4878104-kat">Kat</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4878104-kat?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4878104-kat?shelf=merciless-cliffhanger">merciless-cliffhanger</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4878104-kat?shelf=war-and-military">war-and-military</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4878104-kat?shelf=high-fantasy">high-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4878104-kat?shelf=freefic">freefic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4878104-kat?shelf=political-intrigues">political-intrigues</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4878104-kat?shelf=my-goddamn-emotions">my-goddamn-emotions</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4878104-kat?shelf=captives-and-slaves">captives-and-slaves</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4878104-kat?shelf=glbt">glbt</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4878104-kat?shelf=m-m">m-m</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer482216963" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9596062718894870536"><b>2016 reread</b><br/><br/>I feared that 2016 me would possibly be less impressed with this series the second time around. Little did I know that I'd read until 3 AM to finish this book this last night, which is rare for a reread. It's even better than I remembered. <br/> <br/><b>2012 review</b><br/><br/>M/m romance has not only become an addiction, it also opens all these little doors inside my head to different scenario's for my favorite books and films. For example, imagine how exciting it would've been if <i>Lord of the Rings</i> Strider di</span>
  <span id="freeText9596062718894870536" style="display:none"><b>2016 reread</b><br /><br />I feared that 2016 me would possibly be less impressed with this series the second time around. Little did I know that I'd read until 3 AM to finish this book this last night, which is rare for a reread. It's even better than I remembered. <br /> <br /><b>2012 review</b><br /><br />M/m romance has not only become an addiction, it also opens all these little doors inside my head to different scenario's for my favorite books and films. For example, imagine how exciting it would've been if <i>Lord of the Rings</i> Strider did not go home to an Arwen? If ya know what I mean...<br /><br />I'm sure there's LOTR fan fiction out there already though, ha!<br /><br />In Damen I recognize that noble Strider type of hero as well. He's a man who is made to be a king. Loyal, honorable, courageous and a warrior extraordinaire. He's the perfect character for a compelling high fantasy tale. Prince Laurent and I, on the other hand, got off on the wrong foot because of what he did to Damen. And in my mind I created numerous scenario's, all ending in his satisfyingly painful death. With him Freece/Pacat (take your pick) took her time to create a complex and intriguing character. Infused with political intrigue and conspiracies from a very early age, it is impossible for Laurent to trust anyone. Therefore it's magnificent to read how these two men slowly form a fragile bond, that finally results in...ahh! <br /><br />Add deadly royal games, spectacular battles and military strategies to <i>Captive Prince</i> and hey, I'm off to cloud nine! <br /><br />But, oh god, what if Laurent finds out who Damen truly is? The thought alone makes me shiver. I'm anticipating book 3 and yet dreading the heartbreak it will cause. It must be worth it though, it will be grand!<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="9596062718894870536" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('UlTShVwhPhTWmMkQljdG28a8pnPICo8fCuN9S8h27U4OO8OO/U+U45CCP3ULaPcu5rFO0BYBtmFe5wLVWESbCQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('vcODt3+3W6lrXPS0I/uk7ktBf1t8lmo6JrEJ9AcrjS7hrJK83tnxXi1GAtG+pBUba0yX+KKdU0RytXZqlxn7aQ==')})
  }
//]]>

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer13240422073072263295">C.S. Pacat is a Melbourne writer. Her first series the <i>Captive Prince</i> trilogy began its life as an original web serial. Self-published in 2013 to critical and commercial success and acclaim, the <i>Captive Prince</i> trilogy was acquired by Penguin, and will be published worldwide in 2015.<br/></span>
